< Text>
Listen to me, guys. I haven't met such a cordial, helpful, polite, friendly, and professional team at ANY car-related establishment, EVER. John is just the greatest guy. He's always so helpful, can diagnose issues with cars so quickly, and gives fair, affordable prices.

My experience with European Auto Service began last year in January when I returned from the holidays and hadn't drove my car for a while. I live nearby and walked up to the shop at 7:45 AM and was greeted by John. I asked him for a jump, which he was more than happy to provide (he walked half a block to my apartment garage to do so with a smile on his face). He even identified I was having an issue with my trunk latch, which HONDA actually MISDIAGNOSED and told me was a sensor issue (for which Honda would not even refund me). John took one look at the problem, sent me a link to order the latch from eBay at an amazing price, and charged a nominal fee to install it. I was blown away at his kindness and his eye for diagnosing the issue. He even replaced my battery at a fraction of the cost that the dealer was charging.

A year later, I was having issues with my door handle getting stuck. I texted John about this, and before I knew it he had already ordered the part, painted it to match my car, and had it ready to install for me, all within 48 hours.

Folks, if you're having issues with your car, contact John at European Auto to see if he can help before you ask anyone else. This gentleman is simply the best. Even when I move away, I'll be coming back to see these guys for a long time to come.<//Text>

<Text>In my opinion, Animal Health Center is the best vet hospital in the Monterey/ Salinas area. The staff there is extremely friendly and welcoming. They also have an entire team of veterinarians with various specialties and expertise, whom are very knowledgeable and their number one priority is to get your pet well. What I like most about Animal Health Center is they are one of the few vets within 100 miles to offer both conventional and natural treatments. I have been taking my 11 year-old handicapped pug, Piglette there for nearly 2 years now. All of the treatments (laser therapy and water therapy) and remedies Piglette received has had very positive results in improving her quality of life. The other thing I like about Animal Health Center is they offer high quality pet food brands that you either cannot find or are hard to find at pet/ grocery stores. Recently they just opened a new location in Seaside which I would say is worth checking out too. I have been to a handful of other vets in the area and none of the others offered the variety of treatments or level care for my pug as Animal Health Center.</Text>< Time>

< text>
I recently completed the purchase of a 2019 Honda CR-V from Berkeley Honda.

Put simply, they took great care of my wife and I from our initial contact through the end of the process. Specifically, I would like to call out owner Tim Beinke and internet manager Brent Miletich.

Brent was our main point of contact throughout the transaction and, really, I could have asked no more of him. After much pondering, my wife and I narrowed our potential color choices down to 3 interior/exterior "finalists." One was white, but the other two were "riskier" choices (not your basic grey/silver/white) and Brent went out of his way to let us see an example of each choice. Once we made our ultimate decision, Brent patiently and carefully went over the post-purchase setup details (all the electronics settings, pairing phones, etc.) and sent us off in style.

As mentioned, we made a specific choice of what we wanted, rather than a simple selection from existing inventory. Owner Tim Beinke got involved in the process, found the exact car we were looking for at another dealership, and did all the behind the scenes stuff to get that specific vehicle faster than I ever thought possible. And, he worked with us to get a more than fair price.

In summary, we got exactly what we wanted at a very fair price. Not sure what more one can ask.</text>

107070585841296094303< /user_id>
<Pictures>None<//Pictures>< review>
Came here with a friend and was excited because I've been really digging the Chinese Noodle Soup places which offer a wholly different flavor than the classic Viet soups I am used to. When I came in, the ordering is done on an iPad attached to a stand and the menu was initially being displayed in Chinese.  Thankfully, there was an English button option and once finished, the waiter comes and takes the tablet.  I chose a pork soup and there were 2 sizes to choose from, and 3 kinds of noodle.  These were thin. rice, and Pho which I thought was odd since at least 2 of these are rice noodles.  I wanted wide and flat so I went with Pho and my friend ordered thin.  When the soups came out I was surprised to see that the Pho was thinner than I had hoped, and her "thin" noodles looked a lot like Bun Bo Hue noodles which are actually thicker and round.  Go figure.  The soup had an interesting flavor that was what I would call notably Chinese.  No idea how to explain it other than that.  The broth was very salty.  My friend and I have a running joke where she never drinks the noodle soup broth and I always do, but this was so salty, she had to order some hot water on the side to dilute it and recommended I do the same.  I initially wanted to pass, but decided I had better.  Now, if you love salty broth, this is probably the saltiest I have ever tasted anywhere.  Not going to say if it is good or bad, but i twas not to my preference and the additional hot water made it edible, and I could not even really drink the soup at all.  The flavor was fine, and memorable, but I found myself just trying to finish to get through the saltiness.  I don't think I would come back unless I was with someone who wanted to try it, in which case I would not necessarily decline, but I would warn them about the saltiness and I would look for a non soup dish my next round.   This is not a bad place, I just felt the soup I ordered was more of a challenge than it was a meal I could enjoy.</review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
If you want a new system, or a repair on your old system, Roland does it all, and they do it very well. They are very professional, with specialists who handle design, parts ordering, scheduling, financing, and installation. They aren‚Äôt the cheapest around, but we appreciated that there is a whole team involved, along with a physical location, and they know what they are doing.

We purchased a new 5 ton Lennox dual zoned unit last fall that we have been very happy with. We later had them install a high quality air scrubber to add to the dust/virus filtration system present in the Lennox unit. They also upgraded all our ducting for energy conservation and efficiency, and they did a fantastic job. Unfortunately we had a power surge this month that seriously damaged the 9 month old unit. Unbelievably, surge protectors don‚Äôt automatically come with HVAC systems. Do yourself a favor and pay a few hundred dollars extra for HVAC surge protectors! We were lucky that we were still under warranty or we would have been out MAJOR money.

We‚Äôve had quite a few employees here, and we have been happy with all of them. They all wore masks and booties and cleaned up after themselves.

My only complaint about Roland is the wait time. This happens with popular businesses, but I feel the waits were excessive- especially for an established customer. It took 3 trips total to repair our unit, which I expected due to parts, but lengthy waits after parts have arrived is excessive, in my opinion, once a repair has been started.

The surge damaged our unit on July 1, and the repair was completed on July 16, but the original completion date was July 20- which would have been 6 days after they received the last part. Almost all of those days were triple digit temps, which led to me becoming ill when the outside temp reached 116¬∞, so they amended the completion date to 2 days after receiving the last part, which was a more reasonable time frame. We purchased a very expensive unit from Roland and also purchased a service contract. We expected much better response times.

Despite my issue with response times, I still recommend this business. Their skill and knowledge is apparent, and I have experienced far too many HVAC technicians who did not have those skills.</Review>

< text>
Dear Mr. Rowland,

I am customer of your company since March 2019, when I had my AC system, furnace, and ducting done. I went through Lowe's and spent over $11,000 for overhauling the whole system. Your guys did a great job and we were very pleased with the install.

However, 1 year and 5 months later, my AC system goes out and here's where things have just gone downhill. A technician from Rowland Air came out and did a leak test and found the coil in the attic had been leaking. I was informed the part was under warranty but the labor had expired after 1 year. The cost to replace the coil would be $1600. Not only that, the cost to have done the leak inspection was $323. I paid the $323 and requested the part to be reordered under warranty.

From that point, I contacted Lowe's and all they managed to do was contact Rowland Air and have the $323 I already paid deducted from the $1600. I think this is standard business practice whether it's a car repair or home repair to absorb the cost of the initial inspection as part of the labor cost for repair/replacement, so it really didn't seem like they did anything. Lowe's then advised me to contact Lennox, who was the manufacturer of this AC system, to see what they could do to help with the labor costs.

I went ahead and contacted Lennox waiting on hold for over an hour and finally when I spoke to someone, I was told the part was made by a sister company, ADP, and was directed to call them. I called ADP and left a voicemail and heard back a few days later saying they could not do anything for labor. I reached out to Lowe's again and have basically been told there is nothing more they can do.

I called Rowland Air's office this past Saturday and vented my frustration with this lack of customer service. I felt that I shouldn't be the one having to call around everywhere and it should be Rowland Air that provides customer service to me as their customer. I was told no one from management was available and she'd take a message and get back to me. Today is Wednesday night and I have yet to receive any callback from your office.

At this point, I have the coil replacement scheduled for 9/10 with Rowland Air. As much as I hate to do this and leave a bad review (which I rarely do), there seems to be no other way to get any help in customer service from Rowland Air. How can a company with contracts from Costco and Lowe's treat their customer this way? I've spent over $11,000 just 1 year and 5 months ago and I'm left to pay this $1600 out of my own pocket? That's not what customer service is about. The reason I went with Lowe's and Rowland Air was because I thought if I ran into a situation like this, there would be excellent customer service willing and ready to take care of me. Instead, I'm left disappointed by your company's lack of service.

It's unfortunate it has come to this, but you've essentially lost me as a customer. Once I get the coil replacement done and pay another $1300 on top of the $300 I've already paid, I'll be taking my business elsewhere and will have to recommend others (family, friends, and neighbors) to do the same, because I would not anyone else to run into the same situation I'm in after paying so much money to a company to install and overhaul the whole system and be asked to pay the labor for part that broke just 1 year and 5 months (probably earlier since it was a leak).

I don't know if I will even get a reply, but as I've said, I feel like I have no other options left.</text>

Sales Guy:  He was courteous, listened to what my wife and I were looking for, provided advice and did a good job.

Installers:  They showed up within the hours provided by our appointment.  They put down drop clothes to protect our carpet from upstairs to the front door. They pointed out important features of our new system such as where the drain line drained into one of our sinks and provided a lot of good information. The company in general.  They provided a portable AC unit free of charge for our 1 night without AC (The sales guys informed us this was possible to get during the day when our system was down, but he also told us we would have AC back on at the end of the first day.  The only AC we had was the portable, so I'd have been very unhappy if this hadn't happened).

All in All, they did a great job and I was very happy.  My only negatives are as follows:
There were a couple of times over the 2 days where they left the front door open.  I never said anything about it, just closed it when this happened. We had a wonderful experience with Rowland.  We bought our home recently and the original system seemed wrong and wasteful.  The home didn't appear to cool/heat right no matter our strategy, electric bills always high even if used only at night, and bedroom cooling seemed weak. We didn't know what was wrong and thought it was normal so we stopped over at Costco and met Breann to talk A/C.  She got us all setup with an inspection with Ron and with our tough work schedule Rowland had many ways to accommodate us from inspections to installation and it was so simple and comforting. We went through Costco for a company we could trust and they were transparent on the process and our options.  They did provide simple solutions upfront to our problem, but I elected saving money on bills and invested up front on removing our Frankenstein system and upgrading for a new balanced 2 zone Fernice & A/C units for system operation of bedrooms independant of rest of our home.  We felt in control of the process; Breann stayed the hub throughout and reacted out to us for scheduling, Ron kindly addressed our home issues and setup install, Scot clearly laid out the install plans, and the installers we so clean and considerate with our home.  Oh and the system is so quiet, they said it was going to be noisy but it purrs compared to our last, I feel the air instead of hear it.  It transcends the zones so evenly and cools & heats so efficiently.  The controls are simpler than my last, missing some capability for the phone app, but it's fine our usage was always simple on/off versus scheduled programming (the wall interface has scheduling though).  The controls are very sleek though and easy to navigate, I like the the tiny zone control in my room. Oh and and they walk us through system operation and maintenance, my first home so honestly didn't know how these thing work.  Turns out not much to it, they'll follow up with us for the first year.
